### MutationResolvers

Ƭ **MutationResolvers**<`ContextType`, `ParentType`\>: `Object`

#### Type parameters

| Name | Type |
| :------ | :------ |
| `ContextType` | `any` |
| `ParentType` | extends [`ResolversParentTypes`](types_generatedGraphQLTypes.md#resolversparenttypes)[``"Mutation"``] = [`ResolversParentTypes`](types_generatedGraphQLTypes.md#resolversparenttypes)[``"Mutation"``] |

#### Type declaration

| Name | Type |
| :------ | :------ |
